===== dashboard.js =====

// Dashboard specific JavaScript

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Create charts for dashboard analytics
    createInventoryChart();
    createOrderStatusChart();
    
    // Function to create inventory chart
    function createInventoryChart() {
        const inventoryChartElement = document.getElementById('inventoryChart');
        if (!inventoryChartElement) return;
        
        // Get data attributes from the chart element
        const productNames = JSON.parse(inventoryChartElement.getAttribute('data-product-names'));
        const quantities = JSON.parse(inventoryChartElement.getAttribute('data-quantities'));
        const minLevels = JSON.parse(inventoryChartElement.getAttribute('data-min-levels'));
        
        const ctx = inventoryChartElement.getContext('2d');
        
        // Create the chart
        const inventoryChart = new Chart(ctx, {
            type: 'bar',
            data: {
                labels: productNames,
                datasets: [
                    {
                        label: 'Current Stock',
                        data: quantities,
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(54, 162, 235, 0.7)',
                        borderColor: 'rgba(54, 162, 235, 1)',
                        borderWidth: 1
                    },
                    {
                        label: 'Minimum Stock Level',
                        data: minLevels,
                        backgroundColor: 'rgba(255, 99, 132, 0.7)',
                        borderColor: 'rgba(255, 99, 132, 1)',
                        borderWidth: 1
                    }
                ]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                scales: {
                    y: {
                        beginAtZero: true,
                        grid: {
                            color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.1)'
                        }
                    },
                    x: {
                        grid: {
                            display: false
                        }
                    }
                },
                plugins: {
                    legend: {
                        position: 'top',
                        labels: {
                            color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.7)'
                        }
                    },
                    title: {
                        display: true,
                        text: 'Inventory Status',
                        color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)',
                        font: {
                            size: 16
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }
    
    // Function to create order status chart
    function createOrderStatusChart() {
        const orderChartElement = document.getElementById('orderStatusChart');
        if (!orderChartElement) return;
        
        // Get data attributes from the chart element
        const statuses = JSON.parse(orderChartElement.getAttribute('data-statuses'));
        const counts = JSON.parse(orderChartElement.getAttribute('data-counts'));
        
        const ctx = orderChartElement.getContext('2d');
        
        // Define colors for different statuses
        const statusColors = {
            'pending': 'rgba(255, 193, 7, 0.8)',
            'processing': 'rgba(23, 162, 184, 0.8)',
            'shipped': 'rgba(13, 110, 253, 0.8)',
            'delivered': 'rgba(40, 167, 69, 0.8)',
            'cancelled': 'rgba(220, 53, 69, 0.8)'
        };
        
        // Map status names to colors
        const backgroundColors = statuses.map(status => statusColors[status.toLowerCase()] || 'rgba(108, 117, 125, 0.8)');
        
        // Create the chart
        const orderChart = new Chart(ctx, {
            type: 'doughnut',
            data: {
                labels: statuses.map(s => s.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + s.slice(1).toLowerCase()),
                datasets: [{
                    data: counts,
                    backgroundColor: backgroundColors,
                    borderColor: 'rgba(24, 24, 24, 1)',
                    borderWidth: 1
                }]
            },
            options: {
                responsive: true,
                maintainAspectRatio: false,
                plugins: {
                    legend: {
                        position: 'right',
                        labels: {
                            color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.7)'
                        }
                    },
                    title: {
                        display: true,
                        text: 'Order Status',
                        color: 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.9)',
                        font: {
                            size: 16
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }
    
    // Update supply chain visualization 
    function updateSupplyChain() {
        const supplyChain = document.querySelector('.supply-chain');
        if (!supplyChain) return;
        
        const activeStep = supplyChain.getAttribute('data-active-step');
        const steps = supplyChain.querySelectorAll('.supply-chain-step');
        
        steps.forEach((step, index) => {
            if (index <= parseInt(activeStep)) {
                step.classList.add('active');
            } else {
                step.classList.remove('active');
            }
        });
    }
    
    // Update low stock warnings
    function updateLowStockWarnings() {
        const lowStockItems = document.querySelectorAll('.low-stock-item');
        if (lowStockItems.length > 0) {
            const lowStockAlert = document.getElementById('low-stock-alert');
            if (lowStockAlert) {
                lowStockAlert.style.display = 'block';
                lowStockAlert.querySelector('.badge').textContent = lowStockItems.length;
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Initialize dashboard components
    updateSupplyChain();
    updateLowStockWarnings();
});


===== image-upload.js =====

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    const dropArea = document.getElementById('drop-area');
    const fileInput = document.getElementById('image');
    const previewContainer = document.getElementById('image-preview-container');
    const previewImage = document.getElementById('image-preview');
    const removeButton = document.getElementById('remove-image');
    
    if (!dropArea || !fileInput) return;
    
    // Prevent default behaviors for drag events
    ['dragenter', 'dragover', 'dragleave', 'drop'].forEach(eventName => {
        dropArea.addEventListener(eventName, preventDefaults, false);
    });
    
    function preventDefaults(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
    }
    
    // Highlight drop area when dragging over it
    ['dragenter', 'dragover'].forEach(eventName => {
        dropArea.addEventListener(eventName, highlight, false);
    });
    
    ['dragleave', 'drop'].forEach(eventName => {
        dropArea.addEventListener(eventName, unhighlight, false);
    });
    
    function highlight() {
        dropArea.classList.add('highlight');
    }
    
    function unhighlight() {
        dropArea.classList.remove('highlight');
    }
    
    // Handle dropped files
    dropArea.addEventListener('drop', handleDrop, false);
    
    function handleDrop(e) {
        const dt = e.dataTransfer;
        const files = dt.files;
        
        if (files.length) {
            fileInput.files = files;
            updatePreview(files[0]);
        }
    }
    
    // Handle file selection via the file input
    fileInput.addEventListener('change', function() {
        if (this.files.length) {
            updatePreview(this.files[0]);
        }
    });
    
    // Handle remove button click
    if (removeButton) {
        removeButton.addEventListener('click', function() {
            fileInput.value = '';
            resetPreview();
        });
    }
    
    // Update the image preview
    function updatePreview(file) {
        // Check if the file is an image
        if (!file.type.match('image.*')) {
            alert('Please select an image file (jpg, png, gif)');
            resetPreview();
            return;
        }
        
        // File size validation (max 2MB)
        if (file.size > 2 * 1024 * 1024) {
            alert('File is too large. Maximum file size is 2MB.');
            resetPreview();
            return;
        }
        
        const reader = new FileReader();
        
        reader.addEventListener('load', function() {
            // Show the preview image
            previewImage.src = reader.result;
            previewContainer.style.display = 'block';
            dropArea.classList.add('has-preview');
            
            // Show the remove button
            if (removeButton) {
                removeButton.style.display = 'block';
            }
        });
        
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    }
    
    // Reset the preview
    function resetPreview() {
        previewImage.src = '';
        previewContainer.style.display = 'none';
        dropArea.classList.remove('has-preview');
        
        // Hide the remove button
        if (removeButton) {
            removeButton.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
    
    // Initialize preview for existing images (for edit form)
    const existingImage = document.getElementById('existing-image');
    if (existingImage && existingImage.getAttribute('data-image-path')) {
        previewImage.src = existingImage.getAttribute('data-image-path');
        previewContainer.style.display = 'block';
        dropArea.classList.add('has-preview');
        if (removeButton) {
            removeButton.style.display = 'block';
        }
    }
});

===== inventory.js =====

// Inventory management specific JavaScript

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Update inventory table styling
    const inventoryTable = document.getElementById('inventory-table');
    if (inventoryTable) {
        const rows = inventoryTable.querySelectorAll('tbody tr');
        
        rows.forEach(row => {
            const quantityCell = row.querySelector('.quantity-cell');
            const minLevelCell = row.querySelector('.min-level-cell');
            
            if (quantityCell && minLevelCell) {
                const quantity = parseInt(quantityCell.textContent);
                const minLevel = parseInt(minLevelCell.textContent);
                
                if (quantity <= 0) {
                    row.classList.add('out-of-stock');
                } else if (quantity < minLevel) {
                    row.classList.add('low-stock');
                }
            }
        });
    }
    
    // Add inventory form validation
    const inventoryForm = document.getElementById('inventory-form');
    if (inventoryForm) {
        inventoryForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            const quantityInput = document.getElementById('quantity');
            const minStockInput = document.getElementById('min_stock_level');
            
            const quantity = parseInt(quantityInput.value);
            const minStock = parseInt(minStockInput.value);
            
            let isValid = true;
            
            if (isNaN(quantity) || quantity < 0) {
                setInputError(quantityInput, 'Quantity must be a positive number');
                isValid = false;
            } else {
                clearInputError(quantityInput);
            }
            
            if (isNaN(minStock) || minStock < 1) {
                setInputError(minStockInput, 'Minimum stock level must be at least 1');
                isValid = false;
            } else {
                clearInputError(minStockInput);
            }
            
            if (!isValid) {
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        });
    }
    
    // Filter inventory table
    const inventoryFilter = document.getElementById('inventory-filter');
    if (inventoryFilter) {
        inventoryFilter.addEventListener('input', function() {
            const filterText = this.value.toLowerCase();
            const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#inventory-table tbody tr');
            
            rows.forEach(row => {
                const productName = row.querySelector('.product-name').textContent.toLowerCase();
                const sku = row.querySelector('.sku').textContent.toLowerCase();
                
                if (productName.includes(filterText) || sku.includes(filterText)) {
                    row.style.display = '';
                } else {
                    row.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        });
    }
    
    // Sort inventory table
    const sortableHeaders = document.querySelectorAll('#inventory-table th.sortable');
    sortableHeaders.forEach(header => {
        header.addEventListener('click', function() {
            const table = document.getElementById('inventory-table');
            const tbody = table.querySelector('tbody');
            const rows = Array.from(tbody.querySelectorAll('tr'));
            
            // Get the column index to sort by
            const index = Array.from(header.parentNode.children).indexOf(header);
            
            // Get the current sort direction or default to ascending
            const direction = header.getAttribute('data-sort-direction') === 'asc' ? 'desc' : 'asc';
            
            // Update all headers to show they're not sorted
            sortableHeaders.forEach(h => {
                h.removeAttribute('data-sort-direction');
                h.querySelector('svg.sort-icon')?.remove();
            });
            
            // Update this header to show it's sorted
            header.setAttribute('data-sort-direction', direction);
            
            // Add the appropriate sort icon
            const sortIcon = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'svg');
            sortIcon.setAttribute('class', 'sort-icon ms-1');
            sortIcon.setAttribute('width', '12');
            sortIcon.setAttribute('height', '12');
            sortIcon.setAttribute('viewBox', '0 0 16 16');
            
            const iconPath = document.createElementNS('http://www.w3.org/2000/svg', 'path');
            if (direction === 'asc') {
                iconPath.setAttribute('d', 'M8 4a.5.5 0 0 1 .5.5v5.793l2.146-2.147a.5.5 0 0 1 .708.708l-3 3a.5.5 0 0 1-.708 0l-3-3a.5.5 0 1 1 .708-.708L7.5 10.293V4.5A.5.5 0 0 1 8 4z');
            } else {
                iconPath.setAttribute('d', 'M8 12a.5.5 0 0 0 .5-.5v-5.793l2.146 2.147a.5.5 0 0 0 .708-.708l-3-3a.5.5 0 0 0-.708 0l-3 3a.5.5 0 1 0 .708.708L7.5 5.707V11.5a.5.5 0 0 0 .5.5z');
            }
            
            sortIcon.appendChild(iconPath);
            header.appendChild(sortIcon);
            
            // Sort the rows
            rows.sort((a, b) => {
                let aValue = a.cells[index].textContent.trim();
                let bValue = b.cells[index].textContent.trim();
                
                // If values are numbers, convert them for numeric sorting
                if (!isNaN(aValue) && !isNaN(bValue)) {
                    aValue = parseFloat(aValue);
                    bValue = parseFloat(bValue);
                }
                
                if (direction === 'asc') {
                    if (aValue < bValue) return -1;
                    if (aValue > bValue) return 1;
                    return 0;
                } else {
                    if (aValue < bValue) return 1;
                    if (aValue > bValue) return -1;
                    return 0;
                }
            });
            
            // Reattach the sorted rows
            rows.forEach(row => tbody.appendChild(row));
        });
    });
    
    // Helper functions for form validation
    function setInputError(input, message) {
        const formControl = input.parentElement;
        const errorElement = formControl.querySelector('.invalid-feedback') || document.createElement('div');
        errorElement.className = 'invalid-feedback';
        errorElement.textContent = message;
        
        input.classList.add('is-invalid');
        if (!formControl.querySelector('.invalid-feedback')) {
            formControl.appendChild(errorElement);
        }
    }
    
    function clearInputError(input) {
        input.classList.remove('is-invalid');
    }
});


===== main.js =====

// Main JS file for inventory management system

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Initialize tooltips
    const tooltipTriggerList = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="tooltip"]'));
    const tooltipList = tooltipTriggerList.map(function(tooltipTriggerEl) {
        return new bootstrap.Tooltip(tooltipTriggerEl);
    });

    // Initialize popovers
    const popoverTriggerList = [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll('[data-bs-toggle="popover"]'));
    const popoverList = popoverTriggerList.map(function(popoverTriggerEl) {
        return new bootstrap.Popover(popoverTriggerEl);
    });

    // Get notification count periodically
    function updateNotificationCount() {
        fetch('/api/notifications/count')
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                const notificationCount = document.getElementById('notification-count');
                if (notificationCount) {
                    notificationCount.textContent = data.count;
                    if (data.count > 0) {
                        notificationCount.style.display = 'flex';
                    } else {
                        notificationCount.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                }
            })
            .catch(error => console.error('Error fetching notification count:', error));
    }

    // Mark notification as read
    const markAsReadButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.mark-notification-read');
    markAsReadButtons.forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            const notificationId = this.getAttribute('data-notification-id');
            
            fetch(`/notifications/mark_read/${notificationId}`, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                    'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest'
                }
            })
            .then(response => response.json())
            .then(data => {
                if (data.success) {
                    const notificationItem = this.closest('.notification-item');
                    notificationItem.classList.remove('bg-light');
                    this.style.display = 'none';
                    updateNotificationCount();
                }
            })
            .catch(error => console.error('Error marking notification as read:', error));
        });
    });

    // Update stock level indicators
    const stockLevelIndicators = document.querySelectorAll('.stock-level-indicator');
    stockLevelIndicators.forEach(indicator => {
        const quantity = parseInt(indicator.getAttribute('data-quantity'));
        const minLevel = parseInt(indicator.getAttribute('data-min-level'));
        const maxLevel = parseInt(indicator.getAttribute('data-max-level') || (minLevel * 3));
        
        const levelEl = indicator.querySelector('.level');
        const percentage = Math.min((quantity / maxLevel) * 100, 100);
        
        levelEl.style.width = `${percentage}%`;
        
        if (quantity <= 0) {
            levelEl.classList.add('level-danger');
        } else if (quantity < minLevel) {
            levelEl.classList.add('level-warning');
        } else {
            levelEl.classList.add('level-good');
        }
    });

    // Check inventory availability when adding to order
    const quantityInput = document.getElementById('quantity');
    const productSelect = document.getElementById('product_id');
    
    if (quantityInput && productSelect) {
        function checkInventory() {
            const productId = productSelect.value;
            const quantity = quantityInput.value;
            
            if (productId && quantity > 0) {
                fetch(`/api/check_inventory/${productId}/${quantity}`)
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        const stockInfoElement = document.getElementById('stock-info');
                        if (stockInfoElement) {
                            if (data.available) {
                                stockInfoElement.textContent = `Stock available (${data.current_stock} units)`;
                                stockInfoElement.className = 'text-success';
                            } else {
                                stockInfoElement.textContent = `Insufficient stock (${data.current_stock} units available)`;
                                stockInfoElement.className = 'text-danger';
                            }
                        }
                    })
                    .catch(error => console.error('Error checking inventory:', error));
            }
        }
        
        productSelect.addEventListener('change', checkInventory);
        quantityInput.addEventListener('input', checkInventory);
    }

    // Initialize notification count
    updateNotificationCount();
    
    // Update notification count every 60 seconds
    setInterval(updateNotificationCount, 60000);
});


===== orders.js =====

// Orders management specific JavaScript

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Order detail modal
    const orderDetailButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.view-order-details');
    orderDetailButtons.forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', function() {
            const orderId = this.getAttribute('data-order-id');
            const modalBody = document.querySelector('#orderDetailModal .modal-body');
            const modalTitle = document.querySelector('#orderDetailModal .modal-title');
            
            // Set modal to loading state
            modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-4"><div class="spinner-border text-primary" role="status"><span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span></div><p class="mt-2">Loading order details...</p></div>';
            modalTitle.textContent = 'Order Details';
            
            // Fetch order details
            fetch(`/orders/${orderId}`, {
                    headers: {
                        'X-Requested-With': 'XMLHttpRequest' // Mark as AJAX request
                    }
                })
                .then(response => {
                    if (!response.ok) {
                        throw new Error('Network response was not ok');
                    }
                    return response.text();
                })
                .then(html => {
                    // Parse the order details HTML
                    const parser = new DOMParser();
                    const doc = parser.parseFromString(html, 'text/html');
                    const orderDetails = doc.querySelector('.order-details');
                    const orderTitle = doc.querySelector('h1');
                    
                    if (orderDetails) {
                        modalBody.innerHTML = '';
                        modalBody.appendChild(orderDetails.cloneNode(true));
                    } else {
                        modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Error loading order details.</div>';
                    }
                    
                    if (orderTitle) {
                        modalTitle.textContent = orderTitle.textContent;
                    } else {
                        // Use a default title based on the parsed content
                        const h2 = doc.querySelector('h2');
                        if (h2) {
                            modalTitle.textContent = h2.textContent;
                        }
                    }
                })
                .catch(error => {
                    console.error('Error fetching order details:', error);
                    modalBody.innerHTML = '<div class="alert alert-danger">Error loading order details. Please try again.</div>';
                });
        });
    });
    
    // Order status update handlers
    const processOrderButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.process-order');
    processOrderButtons.forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to process this order? This will update inventory levels.')) {
                const form = document.createElement('form');
                form.method = 'POST';
                form.action = this.href;
                
                // Add CSRF token
                const csrfToken = document.querySelector('meta[name="csrf-token"]').getAttribute('content');
                const csrfInput = document.createElement('input');
                csrfInput.type = 'hidden';
                csrfInput.name = 'csrf_token';
                csrfInput.value = csrfToken;
                form.appendChild(csrfInput);
                
                document.body.appendChild(form);
                form.submit();
            }
        });
    });
    
    const completeOrderButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.complete-order');
    completeOrderButtons.forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to mark this order as shipped?')) {
                const form = document.createElement('form');
                form.method = 'POST';
                form.action = this.href;
                document.body.appendChild(form);
                form.submit();
            }
        });
    });
    
    const receiveOrderButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.receive-order');
    receiveOrderButtons.forEach(button => {
        button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            e.preventDefault();
            
            if (confirm('Are you sure you want to mark this order as received? This will update your inventory.')) {
                const form = document.createElement('form');
                form.method = 'POST';
                form.action = this.href;
                document.body.appendChild(form);
                form.submit();
            }
        });
    });
    
    // Supplier selection and form validation
    const orderForm = document.getElementById('order-form');
    const supplierCards = document.querySelectorAll('.supplier-card');
    const supplierRadios = document.querySelectorAll('.supplier-radio');
    const supplierIdField = document.getElementById('supplier_id');
    const submitButton = orderForm?.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
    
    // Handle supplier card selection
    if (supplierCards.length > 0 && supplierIdField) {
        // Initialize select field with choices
        supplierIdField.innerHTML = '';
        supplierCards.forEach(card => {
            const supplierId = card.getAttribute('data-supplier-id');
            const option = document.createElement('option');
            option.value = supplierId;
            option.textContent = supplierId;
            supplierIdField.appendChild(option);
            
            // Make whole card clickable
            card.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (!e.target.classList.contains('supplier-radio')) {
                    const radio = this.querySelector('.supplier-radio');
                    if (radio) {
                        radio.checked = true;
                        
                        // Manually trigger change event
                        const event = new Event('change');
                        radio.dispatchEvent(event);
                    }
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Set the selected supplier when radio button is clicked
        supplierRadios.forEach(radio => {
            radio.addEventListener('change', function() {
                const supplierId = this.value;
                supplierIdField.value = supplierId;
                
                // Highlight the selected card
                supplierCards.forEach(card => {
                    if (card.getAttribute('data-supplier-id') === supplierId) {
                        card.classList.add('border-primary');
                        
                        // Check if this supplier has inventory
                        const hasInventory = !card.querySelector('.text-warning');
                        
                        // Show warning if supplier has no inventory
                        if (!hasInventory && submitButton) {
                            // Add warning beneath the submit button
                            let warningEl = document.getElementById('supplier-warning');
                            if (!warningEl) {
                                warningEl = document.createElement('div');
                                warningEl.id = 'supplier-warning';
                                warningEl.className = 'alert alert-warning mt-2';
                                warningEl.innerHTML = '<i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle me-1"></i> The selected supplier has no products available. You can still place an order, but you won\'t be able to add any items until they stock up.';
                                submitButton.parentNode.appendChild(warningEl);
                            }
                        } else {
                            // Remove warning if exists
                            const warningEl = document.getElementById('supplier-warning');
                            if (warningEl) {
                                warningEl.remove();
                            }
                        }
                    } else {
                        card.classList.remove('border-primary');
                    }
                });
            });
        });
        
        // Initially check first radio if none selected
        if (supplierRadios.length > 0 && !document.querySelector('.supplier-radio:checked')) {
            supplierRadios[0].checked = true;
            
            // Manually trigger change event
            const event = new Event('change');
            supplierRadios[0].dispatchEvent(event);
        }
    }
    
    // Order form validation
    if (orderForm) {
        orderForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            const checkedRadio = document.querySelector('.supplier-radio:checked');
            
            if (!checkedRadio) {
                e.preventDefault();
                alert('Please select a supplier.');
                return false;
            }
            
            // Ensure the supplier_id field is set with the selected value
            supplierIdField.value = checkedRadio.value;
            return true;
        });
    }
    
    // Order items form validation
    const orderItemForm = document.getElementById('order-item-form');
    if (orderItemForm) {
        orderItemForm.addEventListener('submit', function(e) {
            const productSelect = document.getElementById('product_id');
            const quantityInput = document.getElementById('quantity');
            const unitPriceInput = document.getElementById('unit_price');
            
            let isValid = true;
            
            if (!productSelect.value) {
                e.preventDefault();
                alert('Please select a product.');
                isValid = false;
            }
            
            const quantity = parseInt(quantityInput.value);
            if (isNaN(quantity) || quantity < 1) {
                e.preventDefault();
                alert('Please enter a valid quantity (minimum 1).');
                isValid = false;
            }
            
            const unitPrice = parseFloat(unitPriceInput.value);
            if (isNaN(unitPrice) || unitPrice <= 0) {
                e.preventDefault();
                alert('Please enter a valid unit price.');
                isValid = false;
            }
            
            return isValid;
        });
    }
    
    // Order status progression visualization
    function updateOrderStatusProgress() {
        const statusElements = document.querySelectorAll('.order-status-progress');
        statusElements.forEach(statusEl => {
            const currentStatus = statusEl.getAttribute('data-status');
            const statuses = ['pending', 'processing', 'shipped', 'delivered'];
            const currentIndex = statuses.indexOf(currentStatus.toLowerCase());
            
            const progressItems = statusEl.querySelectorAll('.order-status-item');
            progressItems.forEach((item, index) => {
                if (index < currentIndex) {
                    item.classList.add('completed');
                } else if (index === currentIndex) {
                    item.classList.add('active');
                }
            });
        });
    }
    
    // Filter orders tables
    // Incoming orders filter
    const incomingOrderFilter = document.getElementById('incoming-order-filter');
    if (incomingOrderFilter) {
        incomingOrderFilter.addEventListener('input', function() {
            const filterText = this.value.toLowerCase();
            const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#incoming-orders-table tbody tr');
            
            rows.forEach(row => {
                let text = '';
                // Get text content from all cells (except the last one which contains actions)
                for (let i = 0; i < row.cells.length - 1; i++) {
                    text += ' ' + row.cells[i].textContent.toLowerCase();
                }
                
                if (text.includes(filterText)) {
                    row.style.display = '';
                } else {
                    row.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        });
    }
    
    // Outgoing orders filter
    const outgoingOrderFilter = document.getElementById('outgoing-order-filter');
    if (outgoingOrderFilter) {
        outgoingOrderFilter.addEventListener('input', function() {
            const filterText = this.value.toLowerCase();
            const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#outgoing-orders-table tbody tr');
            
            rows.forEach(row => {
                let text = '';
                // Get text content from all cells (except the last one which contains actions)
                for (let i = 0; i < row.cells.length - 1; i++) {
                    text += ' ' + row.cells[i].textContent.toLowerCase();
                }
                
                if (text.includes(filterText)) {
                    row.style.display = '';
                } else {
                    row.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        });
    }
    
    // Legacy support for old filter
    const orderFilter = document.getElementById('order-filter');
    if (orderFilter) {
        orderFilter.addEventListener('input', function() {
            const filterText = this.value.toLowerCase();
            const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#orders-table tbody tr');
            
            rows.forEach(row => {
                const orderNumber = row.querySelector('.order-number')?.textContent.toLowerCase() || '';
                const customer = row.querySelector('.customer-name')?.textContent.toLowerCase() || '';
                const status = row.querySelector('.order-status')?.textContent.toLowerCase() || '';
                
                if (orderNumber.includes(filterText) || customer.includes(filterText) || status.includes(filterText)) {
                    row.style.display = '';
                } else {
                    row.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        });
    }
    
    // Initialize order status progress
    updateOrderStatusProgress();
});

{% block scripts %}
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const productSelect = document.getElementById('product_select');
        const productDetails = document.getElementById('product-details');
        const priceField = document.getElementById('unit_price');
        
        // Product data mapping
        const productData = {
            {% for inv in supplier_inventory %}
            {{ inv.product_id }}: {
                name: "{{ inv.product.name }}",
                category: "{{ inv.product.category }}",
                size: "{{ inv.product.size }}",
                color: "{{ inv.product.color }}",
                pattern: "{{ inv.product.pattern }}",
                gender: "{{ inv.product.gender }}",
                price: {{ inv.product.price }},
                stock: {{ inv.quantity }}
            },
            {% endfor %}
        };
        
        // Set initial unit price if available
        if (productSelect.value && productData[productSelect.value]) {
            priceField.value = productData[productSelect.value].price;
        }
        
        productSelect.addEventListener('change', function() {
            const productId = parseInt(this.value);
            
            // Hide form for "No products available"
            const submitButton = document.querySelector('button[type="submit"]');
            const quantityField = document.getElementById('quantity');
            
            if (productId === 0) {
                // Disable form inputs
                submitButton.disabled = true;
                quantityField.disabled = true;
                priceField.disabled = true;
                
                // Hide product details
                productDetails.classList.add('d-none');
                return;
            } else {
                // Enable form inputs
                submitButton.disabled = false;
                quantityField.disabled = false;
                priceField.disabled = false;
            }
            
            if (productId && productData[productId]) {
                const product = productData[productId];
                
                // Show details card
                productDetails.classList.remove('d-none');
                
                // Update details
                document.getElementById('product-category').textContent = formatCategory(product.category);
                document.getElementById('product-size').textContent = product.size || 'N/A';
                document.getElementById('product-color').textContent = product.color || 'N/A';
                document.getElementById('product-pattern').textContent = product.pattern || 'N/A';
                document.getElementById('product-gender').textContent = formatGender(product.gender);
                document.getElementById('product-stock').textContent = product.stock + ' in stock';
                
                // Set color swatch if available
                if (product.color) {
                    const colorSwatch = document.getElementById('product-color-swatch');
                    colorSwatch.style.backgroundColor = product.color;
                    colorSwatch.style.display = 'inline-block';
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('product-color-swatch').style.display = 'none';
                }
                
                // Set price
                priceField.value = product.price;
            } else {
                productDetails.classList.add('d-none');
                priceField.value = '';
            }
        });
        
        // Helper functions to format display values
        function formatCategory(category) {
            if (category === 'tshirt') return 'T-Shirt';
            if (category === 'shoes') return 'Shoes';
            if (category === 'accessories') return 'Accessories';
            return category;
        }
        
        function formatGender(gender) {
            if (gender === 'mens') return "Men's";
            if (gender === 'womens') return "Women's";
            if (gender === 'unisex') return "Unisex";
            return gender;
        }
        
        // Trigger initial change to populate fields if needed
        const event = new Event('change');
        productSelect.dispatchEvent(event);
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}

                                            data-quantity="{{ item.quantity }}"

                                    </button>
                                </td>
                            </tr>
                            {% endfor %}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
                {% else %}
                <div class="text-center py-5">
                    <i class="fas fa-box-open fa-3x text-muted mb-3"></i>
                    <p>Your inventory is empty.</p>
                    <a href="{{ url_for('place_order') }}" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm">Order Products</a>
                </div>
                {% endif %}
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Populate update inventory modal with product data
        const updateInventoryModal = document.getElementById('updateInventoryModal');
        updateInventoryModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
            const button = event.relatedTarget;
            const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
            const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
            const quantity = button.getAttribute('data-quantity');
            const minLevel = button.getAttribute('data-min-level');
            
            // Update modal form fields
            const modal = this;
            modal.querySelector('#product_id').value = productId;
            modal.querySelector('#product_name').value = productName;
            modal.querySelector('#quantity').value = quantity;
            modal.querySelector('#min_stock_level').value = minLevel;
        });
    });
</script>

    <!-- Chart.js -->
    <script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>
</head>
<body>
    <header>
        <nav class="navbar navbar-expand-lg navbar-dark bg-dark">
            <div class="container-fluid">
                <a class="navbar-brand" href="{{ url_for('index') }}">
                    <i class="fas fa-cubes me-2"></i>SupplyChain
                </a>
                <button class="navbar-toggler" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#navbarMain" aria-controls="navbarMain" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Toggle navigation">
                    <span class="navbar-toggler-icon"></span>

===== order_details.html =====

<div class="order-details">

        <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
            <h2 class="mb-0">Order #{{ order.order_number }}</h2>

                'warning' if order.status == 'pending' else
                'info' if order.status == 'processing' else
                'primary' if order.status == 'shipped' else
                'success' if order.status == 'delivered' else
                'danger'
            }} fs-6">{{ order.status | capitalize }}</span>
        </div>
        <div class="text-muted">
            Placed on {{ order.created_at.strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M') }}
        </div>
    </div>

        <div class="col-md-6">
            <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm h-100">
                <div class="card-body">
                    <h5 class="card-title"><i class="fas fa-user me-2"></i>Customer</h5>
                    <p class="mb-1"><strong>{{ order.customer.username }}</strong></p>
                    <p class="mb-1">{{ order.customer.email }}</p>
                    {% if order.customer.company_name %}
                    <p class="mb-0">{{ order.customer.company_name }}</p>
                    {% endif %}
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        <div class="col-md-6">

                <div class="card-body">
                    <h5 class="card-title"><i class="fas fa-building me-2"></i>Supplier</h5>

                    <p class="mb-1">{{ order.supplier.email }}</p>
                    {% if order.supplier.company_name %}
                    <p class="mb-0">{{ order.supplier.company_name }}</p>
                    {% endif %}
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mb-4">
        <div class="card-header bg-transparent">

        </div>

            <div class="table-responsive">

                                    </small>

                                    </small>
                                    
                                    <small>
                                        <strong>Color:</strong> 
                                        {% if item.product.color %}
                                        <span style="display: inline-block; width: 12px; height: 12px; border-radius: 50%; background-color: {{ item.product.color }}; margin-right: 3px;"></span>
                                        {{ item.product.color }}
                                        {% else %}
                                        N/A
                                        {% endif %}
                                    </small>

                                        <strong>Pattern:</strong> {{ item.product.pattern|product_attr }}
                                    </small>

                    </tbody>
                    <tfoot>
                        <tr>

                            <td><strong>${{ "%.2f"|format(order.total_amount) }}</strong></td>

                </table>
            </div>
        </div>

    <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mb-4">

                                {{ order.updated_at.strftime('%Y-%m-%d') }}
                            {% else %}
                                Pending
                            {% endif %}
                        </small>
                    </div>

                            {% endif %}
                        </small>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    
    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between">
        {% if current_user.id == order.supplier_id and order.status == 'pending' %}
        <form action="{{ url_for('process_order', order_id=order.id) }}" method="post" class="d-inline">
            <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="{{ csrf_token() }}">
            <button type="submit" class="btn btn-success process-order">
                <i class="fas fa-check me-1"></i> Process Order
            </button>
        </form>
        {% elif current_user.id == order.supplier_id and order.status == 'processing' %}
        <form action="{{ url_for('complete_order', order_id=order.id) }}" method="post" class="d-inline">
            <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="{{ csrf_token() }}">
            <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary complete-order">
                <i class="fas fa-shipping-fast me-1"></i> Mark as Shipped
            </button>
        </form>
        {% elif current_user.id == order.customer_id and order.status == 'shipped' %}
        <form action="{{ url_for('receive_order', order_id=order.id) }}" method="post" class="d-inline">
            <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="{{ csrf_token() }}">
            <button type="submit" class="btn btn-success receive-order">
                <i class="fas fa-check me-1"></i> Mark as Received
            </button>
        </form>
        {% else %}
        <div></div>
        {% endif %}
        
        <button type="button" class="btn btn-secondary" data-bs-dismiss="modal">Close</button>
    </div>
</div>

                                        {% set inventory_count = supplier.inventory|selectattr('quantity', 'gt', 0)|list|count %}

                                            <i class="fas fa-check-circle me-1"></i> {{ inventory_count }} products available
                                        </div>
                                        {% endif %}
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            {% endfor %}
                            
                            {% if suppliers|length == 0 %}
                            <div class="col-12">
                                <div class="alert alert-warning">
                                    <i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle me-2"></i>
                                    No suppliers are currently available. Please try again later.
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            {% endif %}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="mb-4">
                        <label for="customer_notes" class="form-label">{{ form.customer_notes.label }}</label>
                        {{ form.customer_notes(class="form-control", rows=3, placeholder="Any special instructions or notes for this order") }}
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="d-grid">
                        {{ form.submit(class="btn btn-primary btn-lg") }}
                    </div>
                </form>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mt-4">
            <div class="card-body">
                <h5 class="card-title">How Ordering Works</h5>
                <div class="order-flow">
                    <div class="order-flow-step active">

{% block scripts %}
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Filter products table
        const productFilter = document.getElementById('product-filter');
        if (productFilter) {
            productFilter.addEventListener('input', function() {
                const filterText = this.value.toLowerCase();
                const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#products-table tbody tr');
                
                rows.forEach(row => {
                    const productName = row.cells[1].textContent.toLowerCase();
                    const category = row.cells[2].textContent.toLowerCase();
                    const gender = row.cells[3].textContent.toLowerCase();
                    
                    if (productName.includes(filterText) || category.includes(filterText) || gender.includes(filterText)) {
                        row.style.display = '';
                    } else {
                        row.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });
            });
        }
        
        // Populate product detail modal
        const productDetailModal = document.getElementById('productDetailModal');
        if (productDetailModal) {
            productDetailModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
                const button = event.relatedTarget;
                const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
                const productSku = button.getAttribute('data-product-sku');
                const productCategory = button.getAttribute('data-product-category');
                const productDescription = button.getAttribute('data-product-description');
                const productSize = button.getAttribute('data-product-size');
                const productColor = button.getAttribute('data-product-color');
                const productPattern = button.getAttribute('data-product-pattern');
                const productGender = button.getAttribute('data-product-gender');
                const productPrice = button.getAttribute('data-product-price');
                const productImage = button.getAttribute('data-product-image');
                
                // Update modal content
                document.getElementById('detail-product-name').textContent = productName;
                document.getElementById('detail-product-sku').textContent = productSku;
                
                // Format category display
                let categoryDisplay = productCategory;
                if (productCategory === 'tshirt') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'T-Shirt';
                } else if (productCategory === 'shoes') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'Shoes';
                } else if (productCategory === 'accessories') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'Accessories';
                } else if (productCategory === 'dress') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'Dress';
                }
                document.getElementById('detail-product-category').textContent = categoryDisplay;
                
                // Format gender display
                let genderDisplay = productGender;
                if (productGender === 'mens') {
                    genderDisplay = "Men's";
                } else if (productGender === 'womens') {
                    genderDisplay = "Women's";
                } else if (productGender === 'unisex') {
                    genderDisplay = "Unisex";
                }
                document.getElementById('detail-product-gender').textContent = genderDisplay;
                
                document.getElementById('detail-product-size').textContent = productSize || 'N/A';
                document.getElementById('detail-product-pattern').textContent = productPattern || 'N/A';
                document.getElementById('detail-product-color').textContent = productColor || 'N/A';
                
                // Set color swatch
                if (productColor) {
                    const colorSwatch = document.getElementById('detail-product-color-swatch');
                    colorSwatch.style.backgroundColor = productColor.startsWith('#') ? productColor : productColor;
                    colorSwatch.style.display = 'inline-block';
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('detail-product-color-swatch').style.display = 'none';
                }
                
                // Format price display
                document.getElementById('detail-product-price').textContent = productPrice ? '$' + parseFloat(productPrice).toFixed(2) : 'N/A';
                
                document.getElementById('detail-product-description').textContent = productDescription || 'No description available';
                
                // Display product image if available
                const productImageElem = document.getElementById('detail-product-image');
                const noImageElem = document.getElementById('detail-product-no-image');
                
                if (productImage) {
                    productImageElem.src = productImage;
                    productImageElem.style.display = 'block';
                    noImageElem.style.display = 'none';
                } else {
                    productImageElem.style.display = 'none';
                    noImageElem.style.display = 'block';
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Populate update inventory modal
        const updateInventoryModal = document.getElementById('updateInventoryModal');
        if (updateInventoryModal) {
            updateInventoryModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
                const button = event.relatedTarget;
                const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
                const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
                
                // Update modal form fields
                this.querySelector('#product_id').value = productId;
                this.querySelector('#product_name').value = productName;
            });
        }
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% extends "layout.html" %}

{% block content %}

                                    <div class="invalid-feedback d-block">{{ error }}</div>
                                {% endfor %}
                            </div>
                        </div>

<div class="row">
    <div class="col-md-12">
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mb-4">
            <div class="card-header bg-transparent">
                <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                    <h5 class="mb-0"><i class="fas fa-boxes me-2"></i>Current Inventory</h5>
                    <div class="input-group w-auto">
                        <span class="input-group-text bg-transparent border-end-0">
                            <i class="fas fa-search"></i>
                        </span>
                        <input type="text" class="form-control border-start-0" id="inventory-filter" placeholder="Search products...">
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="card-body p-0">
                {% if inventory %}
                <div class="table-responsive">
                    <table class="table table-hover mb-0" id="inventory-table">
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="name">Product Name</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="sku">SKU</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="category">Category</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="quantity">Quantity</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="min_level">Min Level</th>
                                <th>Stock Status</th>
                                <th>Actions</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                            {% for item in inventory %}
                            <tr>
                                <td class="product-name">{{ item.product.name }}</td>
                                <td class="sku">{{ item.product.sku }}</td>
                                <td>{{ item.product.category }}</td>
                                <td class="quantity-cell">{{ item.quantity }}</td>
                                <td class="min-level-cell">{{ item.min_stock_level }}</td>
                                <td>
                                    <div class="stock-level-indicator" data-quantity="{{ item.quantity }}" data-min-level="{{ item.min_stock_level }}">
                                        <div class="level"></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <small class="d-block mt-1">
                                        {% if item.quantity <= 0 %}
                                            <span class="text-danger">Out of Stock</span>
                                        {% elif item.quantity < item.min_stock_level %}
                                            <span class="text-warning">Low Stock</span>
                                        {% else %}
                                            <span class="text-success">In Stock</span>
                                        {% endif %}
                                    </small>
                                </td>
                                <td>
                                    <button type="button" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#updateInventoryModal" 
                                            data-product-id="{{ item.product_id }}" 
                                            data-product-name="{{ item.product.name }}" 
                                            data-quantity="{{ item.quantity }}"
                                            data-min-level="{{ item.min_stock_level }}">
                                        <i class="fas fa-edit"></i> Update
                                    </button>
                                </td>
                            </tr>
                            {% endfor %}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
                {% else %}
                <div class="text-center py-5">
                    <i class="fas fa-box-open fa-3x text-muted mb-3"></i>
                    <p>Your inventory is empty.</p>
                    <a href="{{ url_for('add_product') }}" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm">Add Products</a>
                </div>
                {% endif %}
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

                    </div>
                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label for="min_stock_level" class="form-label">Minimum Stock Level</label>

{% block scripts %}
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/inventory.js') }}"></script>
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/dashboard.js') }}"></script>
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Populate update inventory modal with product data
        const updateInventoryModal = document.getElementById('updateInventoryModal');
        updateInventoryModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
            const button = event.relatedTarget;
            const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
            const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
            const quantity = button.getAttribute('data-quantity');
            const minLevel = button.getAttribute('data-min-level');
            
            // Update modal form fields
            const modal = this;
            modal.querySelector('#product_id').value = productId;
            modal.querySelector('#product_name').value = productName;
            modal.querySelector('#quantity').value = quantity;
            modal.querySelector('#min_stock_level').value = minLevel;
        });
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}


===== orders.html =====

{% extends "layout.html" %}

{% block title %}Manufacturer Orders{% endblock %}

{% block content %}
<div class="container-fluid px-4 py-4">
    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-4">
        <div>
            <h1 class="fw-bold">Orders from Wholesalers</h1>
            <p class="text-muted">Manage and fulfill orders from wholesalers</p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <ul class="nav nav-tabs" id="ordersTab" role="tablist">
        <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
            <button class="nav-link active" id="incoming-tab" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#incoming" type="button" role="tab" aria-controls="incoming" aria-selected="true">
                <i class="fas fa-inbox me-1"></i> Incoming Orders (From Wholesalers)
            </button>
        </li>
        <li class="nav-item" role="presentation">
            <button class="nav-link" id="outgoing-tab" data-bs-toggle="tab" data-bs-target="#outgoing" type="button" role="tab" aria-controls="outgoing" aria-selected="false">
                <i class="fas fa-paper-plane me-1"></i> My Outgoing Orders
            </button>
        </li>
    </ul>

    <div class="tab-content mb-4" id="ordersTabContent">
        <div class="tab-pane fade show active" id="incoming" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="incoming-tab">
            <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm border-top-0">
                <div class="card-header bg-transparent py-3">
                    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                        <h5 class="mb-0"><i class="fas fa-clipboard-list me-2"></i>Incoming Orders</h5>
                        <div class="input-group w-auto" style="max-width: 300px;">
                            <span class="input-group-text" id="basic-addon1"><i class="fas fa-search"></i></span>
                            <input type="text" class="form-control" id="incoming-order-filter" placeholder="Search orders...">
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="card-body p-0">
                    {% set incoming_orders = orders|selectattr('supplier_id', 'equalto', current_user.id)|list %}
                    {% if incoming_orders %}
                    <div class="table-responsive">
                        <table class="table table-hover align-middle mb-0" id="incoming-orders-table">
                            <thead>
                                <tr>
                                    <th>Order #</th>
                                    <th>Wholesaler</th>
                                    <th>Date</th>
                                    <th>Status</th>
                                    <th>Items</th>
                                    <th>Total</th>
                                    <th>Actions</th>
                                </tr>
                            </thead>
                            <tbody>
                                {% for order in incoming_orders %}
                                <tr>
                                    <td>{{ order.order_number }}</td>
                                    <td>{{ order.customer.username }}</td>
                                    <td>{{ order.created_at.strftime('%Y-%m-%d') }}</td>
                                    <td>
                                        <span class="badge bg-{{ 
                                            'warning' if order.status == 'pending' else
                                            'info' if order.status == 'processing' else
                                            'primary' if order.status == 'shipped' else
                                            'success' if order.status == 'delivered' else
                                            'danger'
                                        }}">
                                            {{ order.status | capitalize }}
                                        </span>
                                    </td>
                                    <td>{{ order.items|length }} item{% if order.items|length != 1 %}s{% endif %}</td>
                                    <td>${{ "%.2f"|format(order.total_amount) }}</td>
                                    <td>
                                        <div class="btn-group" role="group">
                                            <a href="{{ url_for('view_order', order_id=order.id) }}" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary">
                                                <i class="fas fa-eye"></i> View
                                            </a>
                                            
                                            {% if order.status == 'pending' %}
                                            <form action="{{ url_for('process_order', order_id=order.id) }}" method="post" class="d-inline">
                                                <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="{{ csrf_token() }}">
                                                <button type="submit" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-success">
                                                    <i class="fas fa-check"></i> Process
                                                </button>
                                            </form>
                                            {% elif order.status == 'processing' %}
                                            <form action="{{ url_for('complete_order', order_id=order.id) }}" method="post" class="d-inline">
                                                <input type="hidden" name="csrf_token" value="{{ csrf_token() }}">
                                                <button type="submit" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary">
                                                    <i class="fas fa-shipping-fast"></i> Ship
                                                </button>
                                            </form>
                                            {% endif %}
                                        </div>
                                    </td>
                                </tr>
                                {% endfor %}
                            </tbody>
                        </table>
                    </div>
                    {% else %}
                    <div class="text-center py-5">
                        <div class="py-4">
                            <i class="fas fa-inbox fa-3x text-muted mb-3"></i>
                            <p>No incoming orders have been received yet.</p>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    {% endif %}
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="tab-pane fade" id="outgoing" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="outgoing-tab">
            <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm border-top-0">
                <div class="card-header bg-transparent py-3">

                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                    {% set outgoing_orders = orders|selectattr('customer_id', 'equalto', current_user.id)|list %}

{% block scripts %}
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/orders.js') }}"></script>
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Status filter tabs
        const statusButtons = document.querySelectorAll('[data-status]');
        statusButtons.forEach(button => {
            button.addEventListener('click', function() {
                // Remove active class from all buttons
                statusButtons.forEach(btn => btn.classList.remove('active'));
                
                // Add active class to clicked button
                this.classList.add('active');
                
                const status = this.getAttribute('data-status');
                const activeTabPane = document.querySelector('.tab-pane.active');
                let tableRows;
                
                if (activeTabPane.id === 'incoming') {
                    tableRows = document.querySelectorAll('#incoming-orders-table tbody tr');
                } else {
                    tableRows = document.querySelectorAll('#outgoing-orders-table tbody tr');
                }
                
                tableRows.forEach(row => {
                    if (status === 'all') {
                        row.style.display = '';
                    } else {
                        const statusText = row.querySelector('.badge')?.textContent.trim().toLowerCase() || '';
                        if (statusText.includes(status)) {
                            row.style.display = '';
                        } else {
                            row.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    }
                });
            });
        });
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% block scripts %}
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/dashboard.js') }}"></script>
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Populate update production modal with product data
        const updateProductionModal = document.getElementById('updateProductionModal');
        updateProductionModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
            const button = event.relatedTarget;
            const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
            const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
            const currentQuantity = button.getAttribute('data-current-quantity');
            const minLevel = button.getAttribute('data-min-level');
            
            // Calculate recommended production quantity (2x minimum level)
            const recommendedQuantity = minLevel * 2;
            
            // Update modal form fields
            const modal = this;
            modal.querySelector('#product_id').value = productId;
            modal.querySelector('#product_name').value = productName;
            modal.querySelector('#current_quantity').value = currentQuantity;
            modal.querySelector('#min_level').value = minLevel;
            modal.querySelector('#quantity').value = recommendedQuantity;
            modal.querySelector('#min_stock_level').value = minLevel;
        });
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}

                    <div class="col-md-5 text-center mb-3">
                        <img id="detail-product-image" src="" alt="Product Image" class="img-fluid product-detail-image" style="max-height: 300px; display: none;">
                        <div id="detail-product-no-image" class="bg-light d-flex align-items-center justify-content-center" style="height: 300px; display: none;">
                            <i class="fas fa-image fa-4x text-muted"></i>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="col-md-7">
                        <h4 id="detail-product-name" class="mb-3"></h4>
                        <div class="mb-3">
                            <span class="badge bg-primary" id="detail-product-category"></span>
                            <span class="badge bg-secondary" id="detail-product-gender"></span>
                            <span class="badge bg-info text-dark" id="detail-product-size"></span>
                        </div>
                        <p class="mb-1"><strong>SKU:</strong> <span id="detail-product-sku"></span></p>
                        <p class="mb-1"><strong>Price:</strong> <span id="detail-product-price"></span></p>
                        <div class="mb-3">
                            <p class="mb-1"><strong>Color:</strong> 
                                <span id="detail-product-color"></span>
                                <span id="detail-product-color-swatch" class="color-swatch d-none" style="width: 15px; height: 15px; display: inline-block; border-radius: 50%; margin-left: 5px;"></span>
                            </p>
                            <p class="mb-1"><strong>Pattern:</strong> <span id="detail-product-pattern"></span></p>
