{% block scripts %}
<script src="https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/chart.js"></script>
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Filter products table
        const productFilter = document.getElementById('product-filter');
        if (productFilter) {
            productFilter.addEventListener('input', function() {
                const filterText = this.value.toLowerCase();
                const rows = document.querySelectorAll('#products-table tbody tr');
                
                rows.forEach(row => {
                    const productName = row.cells[1]?.textContent.toLowerCase() || '';
                    const category = row.cells[2]?.textContent.toLowerCase() || '';
                    const gender = row.cells[3]?.textContent.toLowerCase() || '';
                    const sku = row.cells[4]?.textContent.toLowerCase() || '';
                    
                    if (productName.includes(filterText) || 
                        category.includes(filterText) || 
                        gender.includes(filterText) ||
                        sku.includes(filterText)) {
                        row.style.display = '';
                    } else {
                        row.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                });
            });
        }
        
        // Populate product detail modal
        const productDetailModal = document.getElementById('productDetailModal');
        if (productDetailModal) {
            productDetailModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
                const button = event.relatedTarget;
                const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
                const productSku = button.getAttribute('data-product-sku');
                const productCategory = button.getAttribute('data-product-category');
                const productDescription = button.getAttribute('data-product-description');
                const productSize = button.getAttribute('data-product-size');
                const productColor = button.getAttribute('data-product-color');
                const productPattern = button.getAttribute('data-product-pattern');
                const productGender = button.getAttribute('data-product-gender');
                const productPrice = button.getAttribute('data-product-price');
                const productImage = button.getAttribute('data-product-image');
                const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
                
                // Update modal content
                document.getElementById('detail-product-name').textContent = productName;
                document.getElementById('detail-product-sku').textContent = productSku;
                
                // Format category display
                let categoryDisplay = productCategory;
                if (productCategory === 'tshirt') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'T-Shirt';
                } else if (productCategory === 'shoes') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'Shoes';
                } else if (productCategory === 'accessories') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'Accessories';
                } else if (productCategory === 'dress') {
                    categoryDisplay = 'Dress';
                }
                document.getElementById('detail-product-category').textContent = categoryDisplay;
                
                // Format gender display
                let genderDisplay = productGender;
                if (productGender === 'mens') {
                    genderDisplay = "Men's";
                } else if (productGender === 'womens') {
                    genderDisplay = "Women's";
                } else if (productGender === 'unisex') {
                    genderDisplay = "Unisex";
                }
                document.getElementById('detail-product-gender').textContent = genderDisplay;
                
                document.getElementById('detail-product-size').textContent = productSize || 'N/A';
                document.getElementById('detail-product-pattern').textContent = productPattern || 'N/A';
                document.getElementById('detail-product-color').textContent = productColor || 'N/A';
                
                // Set color swatch
                if (productColor) {
                    const colorSwatch = document.getElementById('detail-product-color-swatch');
                    colorSwatch.style.backgroundColor = productColor;
                    colorSwatch.classList.remove('d-none');
                } else {
                    document.getElementById('detail-product-color-swatch').classList.add('d-none');
                }
                
                // Format price display
                document.getElementById('detail-product-price').textContent = productPrice ? '$' + parseFloat(productPrice).toFixed(2) : 'N/A';
                
                document.getElementById('detail-product-description').textContent = productDescription || 'No description available';
                
                // Display product image if available
                const productImageElem = document.getElementById('detail-product-image');
                const noImageElem = document.getElementById('detail-product-no-image');
                
                if (productImage) {
                    productImageElem.src = productImage;
                    productImageElem.style.display = 'block';
                    noImageElem.style.display = 'none';
                } else {
                    productImageElem.style.display = 'none';
                    noImageElem.style.display = 'flex';
                }

                // Set edit link
                if (productId) {
                    document.getElementById('edit-product-link').href = `/products/edit/${productId}`;
                }
            });
        }
        
        // Populate update inventory modal
        const updateInventoryModal = document.getElementById('updateInventoryModal');
        if (updateInventoryModal) {
            updateInventoryModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
                const button = event.relatedTarget;
                const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
                const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
                
                // Update modal form fields
                this.querySelector('#product_id').value = productId;
                this.querySelector('#product_name').value = productName;
            });
        }

        // Create category chart
        try {
            // Extract data from products directly in JavaScript
            const categoryData = {};
            const genderData = {};
            
            // Get all products from the table
            const productRows = document.querySelectorAll('#products-table tbody tr:not([style*="display: none"])');
            
            productRows.forEach(row => {
                if (row.cells.length > 2) { // Make sure it's a valid product row
                    const category = row.cells[2].textContent.trim().toLowerCase();
                    const gender = row.cells[3].textContent.trim().toLowerCase();
                    
                    // Process categories
                    const categoryKey = category === 't-shirt' ? 'tshirt' : 
                                       category === 'shoes' ? 'shoes' : 
                                       category === 'accessories' ? 'accessories' : 
                                       category === 'dress' ? 'dress' : category;
                    
                    if (!categoryData[categoryKey]) {
                        categoryData[categoryKey] = 0;
                    }
                    categoryData[categoryKey]++;
                    
                    // Process genders
                    const genderKey = gender === "men's" ? 'mens' : 
                                     gender === "women's" ? 'womens' : 
                                     gender === 'unisex' ? 'unisex' : gender;
                    
                    if (!genderData[genderKey]) {
                        genderData[genderKey] = 0;
                    }
                    genderData[genderKey]++;
                }
            });

            // Format category names
            const categoryLabels = {
                'tshirt': 'T-Shirts',
                'shoes': 'Shoes',
                'accessories': 'Accessories',
                'dress': 'Dresses'
            };

            // Format gender names
            const genderLabels = {
                'mens': "Men's",
                'womens': "Women's",
                'unisex': 'Unisex'
            };

            // Create chart for categories
            const categoryCtx = document.getElementById('category-chart');
            if (categoryCtx) {
                new Chart(categoryCtx, {
                    type: 'doughnut',
                    data: {
                        labels: Object.keys(categoryData).map(key => categoryLabels[key] || key),
                        datasets: [{
                            data: Object.values(categoryData),
                            backgroundColor: [
                                '#4e73df', 
                                '#1cc88a', 
                                '#36b9cc',
                                '#f6c23e'
                            ],
                            hoverOffset: 4
                        }]
                    },
                    options: {
                        responsive: true,
                        plugins: {
                            legend: {
                                position: 'right',
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            }

            // Create chart for genders
            const genderCtx = document.getElementById('gender-chart');
            if (genderCtx) {
                new Chart(genderCtx, {
                    type: 'doughnut',
                    data: {
                        labels: Object.keys(genderData).map(key => genderLabels[key] || key),
                        datasets: [{
                            data: Object.values(genderData),
                            backgroundColor: [
                                '#1cc88a', 
                                '#4e73df', 
                                '#f6c23e'
                            ],
                            hoverOffset: 4
                        }]
                    },
                    options: {
                        responsive: true,
                        plugins: {
                            legend: {
                                position: 'right',
                            }
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Error creating charts:", e);
        }
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}

{% extends "layout.html" %}

{% block content %}
<div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-4">
    <div>
        <h1 class="fw-bold">Inventory Management</h1>
        <p class="text-muted">Manage your retail store inventory</p>

        <a href="{{ url_for('place_order') }}" class="btn btn-primary">
            <i class="fas fa-plus me-1"></i> Order New Stock

<div class="row">
    <div class="col-md-12">
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mb-4">
            <div class="card-header bg-transparent">
                <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                    <h5 class="mb-0"><i class="fas fa-boxes me-2"></i>Current Inventory</h5>
                    <div class="input-group w-auto">
                        <span class="input-group-text bg-transparent border-end-0">
                            <i class="fas fa-search"></i>
                        </span>
                        <input type="text" class="form-control border-start-0" id="inventory-filter" placeholder="Search products...">
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="card-body p-0">

                <div class="table-responsive">
                    <table class="table table-hover mb-0" id="inventory-table">
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="name">Product Name</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="sku">SKU</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="category">Category</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="quantity">Quantity</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="min_level">Min Level</th>
                                <th>Stock Status</th>
                                <th>Actions</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                            {% for item in inventory %}
                            <tr>
                                <td class="product-name">{{ item.product.name }}</td>
                                <td class="sku">{{ item.product.sku }}</td>
                                <td>{{ item.product.category }}</td>
                                <td class="quantity-cell">{{ item.quantity }}</td>
                                <td class="min-level-cell">{{ item.min_stock_level }}</td>
                                <td>
                                    <div class="stock-level-indicator" data-quantity="{{ item.quantity }}" data-min-level="{{ item.min_stock_level }}">
                                        <div class="level"></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <small class="d-block mt-1">
                                        {% if item.quantity <= 0 %}
                                            <span class="text-danger">Out of Stock</span>
                                        {% elif item.quantity < item.min_stock_level %}
                                            <span class="text-warning">Low Stock</span>
                                        {% else %}
                                            <span class="text-success">In Stock</span>
                                        {% endif %}
                                    </small>
                                </td>
                                <td>
                                    <button type="button" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#updateInventoryModal" 
                                            data-product-id="{{ item.product_id }}" 
                                            data-product-name="{{ item.product.name }}" 
                                            data-quantity="{{ item.quantity }}"
                                            data-min-level="{{ item.min_stock_level }}">
                                        <i class="fas fa-edit"></i> Update
                                    </button>
                                </td>
                            </tr>
                            {% endfor %}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
                {% else %}
                <div class="text-center py-5">
                    <i class="fas fa-box-open fa-3x text-muted mb-3"></i>
                    <p>Your inventory is empty.</p>
                    <a href="{{ url_for('place_order') }}" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm">Order Products</a>
                </div>
                {% endif %}
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<!-- Update Inventory Modal -->
<div class="modal fade" id="updateInventoryModal" tabindex="-1" aria-labelledby="updateInventoryModalLabel" aria-hidden="true">
    <div class="modal-dialog">
        <div class="modal-content">
            <div class="modal-header">
                <h5 class="modal-title" id="updateInventoryModalLabel">Update Inventory</h5>
                <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close"></button>
            </div>

                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label for="product_name" class="form-label">Product</label>
                        <input type="text" class="form-control" id="product_name" readonly>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label for="quantity" class="form-label">Quantity</label>
                        <input type="number" class="form-control" id="quantity" name="quantity" min="0" required>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label for="min_stock_level" class="form-label">Minimum Stock Level</label>
                        <input type="number" class="form-control" id="min_stock_level" name="min_stock_level" min="1" required>
                        <div class="form-text">You'll receive alerts when stock falls below this level.</div>
                    </div>
                </div>

</div>

{% block scripts %}
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/inventory.js') }}"></script>
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Populate update inventory modal with product data
        const updateInventoryModal = document.getElementById('updateInventoryModal');
        updateInventoryModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
            const button = event.relatedTarget;
            const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
            const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
            const quantity = button.getAttribute('data-quantity');
            const minLevel = button.getAttribute('data-min-level');
            
            // Update modal form fields
            const modal = this;
            modal.querySelector('#product_id').value = productId;
            modal.querySelector('#product_name').value = productName;
            modal.querySelector('#quantity').value = quantity;
            modal.querySelector('#min_stock_level').value = minLevel;
        });
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}

                </div>

            <div class="card-body p-0">
                {% if inventory %}
                <div class="table-responsive">
                    <table class="table table-hover mb-0" id="inventory-table">
                        <thead>
                            <tr>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="name">Product Name</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="sku">SKU</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="category">Category</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="quantity">Quantity</th>
                                <th class="sortable" data-sort-field="min_level">Min Level</th>
                                <th>Stock Status</th>
                                <th>Actions</th>
                            </tr>
                        </thead>
                        <tbody>
                            {% for item in inventory %}
                            <tr>
                                <td class="product-name">{{ item.product.name }}</td>
                                <td class="sku">{{ item.product.sku }}</td>
                                <td>{{ item.product.category }}</td>
                                <td class="quantity-cell">{{ item.quantity }}</td>
                                <td class="min-level-cell">{{ item.min_stock_level }}</td>
                                <td>
                                    <div class="stock-level-indicator" data-quantity="{{ item.quantity }}" data-min-level="{{ item.min_stock_level }}">
                                        <div class="level"></div>
                                    </div>
                                    <small class="d-block mt-1">
                                        {% if item.quantity <= 0 %}
                                            <span class="text-danger">Out of Stock</span>
                                        {% elif item.quantity < item.min_stock_level %}
                                            <span class="text-warning">Low Stock</span>
                                        {% else %}
                                            <span class="text-success">In Stock</span>
                                        {% endif %}
                                    </small>
                                </td>
                                <td>
                                    <button type="button" class="btn btn-sm btn-outline-primary" data-bs-toggle="modal" data-bs-target="#updateInventoryModal" 
                                            data-product-id="{{ item.product_id }}" 
                                            data-product-name="{{ item.product.name }}" 
                                            data-quantity="{{ item.quantity }}"
                                            data-min-level="{{ item.min_stock_level }}">
                                        <i class="fas fa-edit"></i> Update
                                    </button>
                                </td>
                            </tr>
                            {% endfor %}
                        </tbody>
                    </table>
                </div>
                {% else %}
                <div class="text-center py-5">
                    <i class="fas fa-box-open fa-3x text-muted mb-3"></i>
                    <p>Your inventory is empty.</p>
                    <a href="{{ url_for('place_order') }}" class="btn btn-primary btn-sm">Order Products</a>
                </div>
                {% endif %}
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

<div class="row">
    <div class="col-md-6">
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mb-4">
            <div class="card-header bg-transparent">
                <h5 class="mb-0"><i class="fas fa-chart-line me-2"></i>Inventory Analytics</h5>
            </div>
            <div class="card-body">
                <div class="chart-container">
                    <canvas id="inventoryChart" 
                        data-product-names="{{ inventory|map(attribute='product.name')|list|tojson }}"
                        data-quantities="{{ inventory|map(attribute='quantity')|list|tojson }}"
                        data-min-levels="{{ inventory|map(attribute='min_stock_level')|list|tojson }}">
                    </canvas>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="col-md-6">
        <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm mb-4">
            <div class="card-header bg-transparent">
                <h5 class="mb-0"><i class="fas fa-exclamation-triangle me-2 text-warning"></i>Low Stock Items</h5>
            </div>
            <div class="card-body p-0">
                {% set low_stock = inventory|selectattr('quantity', 'le', attribute='min_stock_level')|list %}
                {% if low_stock %}
                <div class="list-group list-group-flush">
                    {% for item in low_stock %}
                    <div class="list-group-item low-stock-item d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                        <div>
                            <div class="fw-medium">{{ item.product.name }}</div>
                            <small class="text-muted">SKU: {{ item.product.sku }}</small>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-center">
                            <div class="fw-bold text-danger">{{ item.quantity }}</div>
                            <small class="text-muted">Min: {{ item.min_stock_level }}</small>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    {% endfor %}
                </div>
                {% else %}
                <div class="text-center py-4">
                    <i class="fas fa-check-circle fa-2x text-success mb-2"></i>
                    <p>No low stock items</p>
                </div>
                {% endif %}
            </div>
            {% if low_stock %}
            <div class="card-footer bg-transparent">
                <div class="d-grid">
                    <a href="{{ url_for('place_order') }}" class="btn btn-warning">Order Stock from Manufacturer</a>
                </div>
            </div>
            {% endif %}
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

                    </div>

                        <input type="number" class="form-control" id="quantity" name="quantity" min="0" required>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mb-3">

{% block scripts %}
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/inventory.js') }}"></script>
<script src="{{ url_for('static', filename='js/dashboard.js') }}"></script>
<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        // Populate update inventory modal with product data
        const updateInventoryModal = document.getElementById('updateInventoryModal');
        updateInventoryModal.addEventListener('show.bs.modal', function (event) {
            const button = event.relatedTarget;
            const productId = button.getAttribute('data-product-id');
            const productName = button.getAttribute('data-product-name');
            const quantity = button.getAttribute('data-quantity');
            const minLevel = button.getAttribute('data-min-level');
            
            // Update modal form fields
            const modal = this;
            modal.querySelector('#product_id').value = productId;
            modal.querySelector('#product_name').value = productName;
            modal.querySelector('#quantity').value = quantity;
            modal.querySelector('#min_stock_level').value = minLevel;
        });
    });
</script>
{% endblock %}
